<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;7.01</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Regulation FD Disclosure. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;11, 2021, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) hosted an analyst day (&#8220;Analyst Day&#8221;). Members of the Company&#8217;s senior leadership team discussed the Company&#8217;s plans to unlock future growth and capture momentum over the next five years. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The event will be accessible via webcast on the Company&#8217;s Investor Relations website at <span style="white-space:nowrap">http://investor.t-mobile.com.</span> A replay of the webcast along with presentation materials will be available on the Investor Relations website at the conclusion of the event. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A copy of the press release relating to the Analyst Day is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information contained in Item 7.01, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>EXHIBIT 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Outlines Supercharged Plan for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> to
Further Extend </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Lead Throughout the 5G Era with Growth in Wireless and Beyond&#133; </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Creating Significant Benefits for Customers and Shareholders </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Analyst Day showcases <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> plans to deliver unmatched network, best customer value and
best experiences in their pursuit to be #1 in customer choice and #1 in customers&#146; hearts </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> offers roadmap to consistently and profitably lead the industry in growth and build for
long-term success by delivering the best 5G network, expanding into a number of addressable markets and deepening customer relationships </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Company shared that it is ahead of plan on merger synergy goals and expects total net present value of merger synergies to be more than
$70&nbsp;billion &#150; up more than 60&nbsp;percent from the original merger guidance of $43&nbsp;billion </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Raises <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-</FONT> and long-term guidance across the board, setting up potential for up to $60&nbsp;billion in shareholder returns from 2023 through 2025 </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>BELLEVUE, Wash. &#150; March</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;11, 2021</B> &#150; In its virtual Analyst Day today, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US,
Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) unveiled ambitious plans to unlock future growth and capture even more momentum over the next five years. Since closing its historic merger with Sprint in April 2020, the Supercharged
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> has delivered industry best total net additions, strong profitability and higher than expected synergies, putting the company on the path to deliver financial results that exceed both the original
three to four-year and longer-term targets provided in the original merger plans. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">line-up</FONT> of some of the
company&#146;s senior executives today, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> outlined plans to use its combination of superior assets and scale from the merger and the recent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">C-Band</FONT> auction,
to continue leading the industry in growth by delivering more value AND the best 5G network combined with the best experiences to consumers and businesses across the country. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Only <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has the superior assets, scale, financial position and customer-loving team to lead this new 5G era
now into the next decade, if not beyond. We are taking that lead and setting our sights higher &#151; taking on new growth ambitions and expanding into new markets like&nbsp;never before. We&#146;re already miles ahead in executing on our clear and
consistent plan, building the fastest, biggest and most available 5G network with the perfect mix of spectrum. That is going to continue to translate into a significant and demonstrable advantage for years to come,&#148; said <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> CEO Mike Sievert. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Better yet, this network and growth is primarily funded by our massive synergies. I am
incredibly proud of our team for driving faster integration and unlocking even more synergies than expected, which will deliver incredible value for our customers and shareholders,&#148; Sievert continued. &#147;We now expect the total net present
value of merger synergies to be more than $70&nbsp;billion &#151; a 60&nbsp;percent jump from our original merger plan. We&#146;ve also raised <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-</FONT> and long-term guidance, setting up the potential to return up
to $60&nbsp;billion to shareholders between 2023 and 2025. The next chapter for this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> is tremendously exciting &#150; and we are truly just hitting our stride!&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Key Event Themes </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Positioned to Maintain 5G Leadership in the 5G Era &#150;
</B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> fastest, biggest and most available 5G network is the foundation on which all of the company&#146;s short- and long-term goals are built. The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-Carrier&#146;s</FONT> superior assets and unrivaled ability to execute has already put the company in the leadership position for 5G and it will continue to drive toward a demonstrable and sustainable 5G
leadership advantage that is expected to last throughout the 5G era and beyond. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">C-band</FONT> Enhances
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> Positioning &#150; </B>While its competitors spent unprecedented totals on the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">C-band</FONT> auction, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> invested
within its financial plan in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">C-band</FONT> to add to its Ultra Capacity 5G. While its Ultra Capacity 5G will have the broadest reach and capacity, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> added <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">C-band</FONT> concentrated on suburban and urban areas, where it will make the biggest impact. This ensures <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> superiority for the 5G era when it comes to quantity, reach and
deployment costs. Securing 40 MHz of spectrum in top markets will augment and complement <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> premier, multi-layer spectrum portfolio, positioning the company for continued leadership and to provide
the best customer experience through the 5G era. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Building the Fastest, Biggest and Most Available 5G Network</B> &#150;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> 5G network build is moving at an unmatched pace, with the company targeting completion by the end of 2023 &#150; just in time for others to get access to their
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">C-band</FONT> spectrum. Competitors will have to spend billions of dollars over years to deploy the spectrum they received, all while <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has been actively putting its
multi-layer spectrum portfolio to work to create the densest and broadest network to benefit American consumers and businesses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is already delivering 5G across more geographic coverage than AT&amp;T and Verizon combined.
Now covering 287&nbsp;million people across 1.6&nbsp;million square miles with 5G, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is the only operator to have deployed dedicated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> spectrum for 5G and
deliver on the true promise of 5G by making ultra-fast speeds averaging 300 megabits per second widely available. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> Ultra Capacity 5G, which uses depth of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> (2.5 GHz), has been rapidly expanding and is covering 125&nbsp;million people today. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Significantly Expanding Addressable Markets &#150; </B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT>
dense network with more spectrum provides capacity and speeds to unlock new growth opportunities. It will take the winning <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-Carrier</FONT> approach and best 5G network to break into new markets, deepen
relationships with customers and take the competition to cable. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Smaller and Rural Markets &#150;</B> There are roughly 50&nbsp;million US households in smaller markets and
rural areas &#150; almost 40&nbsp;percent of all households in America &#150; where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> market share is in the low teens compared to its national average market share of approximately
30&nbsp;percent. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-Carrier</FONT> announced plans to increase to a near 20&nbsp;percent share of these areas over the next five years. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will bring a compelling
value proposition to the most underserved areas by serving consumers with mobile, home broadband, and emerging 5G products &#150; while delivering the best experience in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">market.&nbsp;T-Mobile</FONT> will expand its
physical footprint by&nbsp;building&nbsp;hundreds of new stores&nbsp;in small towns&nbsp;and&nbsp;communities over next five years, including over 200 new stores this year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> products will also be available in nearly 1,000&nbsp;Best Buy stores and more than 2,200
Walmart stores (nearly 1,000 in rural America). It also will introduce Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> products in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> stores in rural America&nbsp;to expand its prepaid reach
and shared plans to open approximately 500 new Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> branded and multi-carrier stores this year to reach new consumers.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Evolving Care and Digital Capabilities &#150;</B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> continues
to provide its customers with world-class service support through its award-winning Team of Experts (TEX) approach. The company shared that in 2021 it will bring the full <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> TEX experience to millions
of legacy Sprint customers, an opportunity to further decrease churn on an accelerated schedule and remove pain points. As that transition is happening, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Retail and Care teams are working together to
improve the experience for these customers, bring them the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> value proposition and move them to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> network. Early Net Promoter Scores from the initial
group of Sprint customers that have completed a full transition are nearly 100&nbsp;percent higher (or 20 points higher) than those who have not migrated. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> announced plans to use simplified digital capabilities to make it easy for customers to
get the help&nbsp;or find the product&nbsp;they need&nbsp;&#150;&nbsp;however,&nbsp;wherever&nbsp;and whenever they need it. This includes enabling&nbsp;effortless purchase&nbsp;of&nbsp;products and service aimed at reducing switching friction,
accelerating self-service and&nbsp;network&nbsp;migration efforts and ensuring its frontline teams in stores and Care are equipped to best take care of customers, creating personalized experiences and getting resolution even faster. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> for Business &#150; </B>Today,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has less than 10&nbsp;percent market share in the large enterprise and government space, and the total business market is more than 50&nbsp;million corporate liable lines &#150; and growing! With <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> 5G leadership, businesses are already making the switch and the growth opportunity is huge. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> expects to DOUBLE its market share in the next five years
to about 20&nbsp;percent, with plenty of room to expand based on strong 2020 performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Home Broadband &#150; </B>Outside of traditional mobile wireless,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> sees a huge opportunity to expand into home broadband. The Company shared plans to bring real competition to the $90&nbsp;billion and growing broadband market. Its initial home broadband pilot had
over 100,000 customers, exceeding expectations. On the heels of its recently announced new home broadband solutions for business, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> is gearing up for its commercial launch of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-home</FONT> broadband for consumers later this month and shared broader plans to expand the service to between seven and eight million broadband customers in five years. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Deepening Customer Relationships &#150;</B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> compelling
value proposition, coupled with the reach and capacity of its leading 5G network, will allow the company a unique opportunity to establish and deepen relationships with consumers, businesses and innovators who value network quality, and who may not
have previously considered the provider.&nbsp;The company&#146;s 5G network leadership allows it to serve customers through enhanced or additional services or devices over time. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will use a
multi-pronged approach to win new accounts and introduce them to its family of mobile offerings &#150; from smartphones, to data devices, to entertainment, home broadband and other new services.</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Unlocking Merger Synergies</B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#150;T-Mobile</FONT> now expects the total
net present value of merger synergies to be more than $70 billion&nbsp;&#150; up more than 60&nbsp;percent from the original merger guidance of $43&nbsp;billion &#150; as the company is unlocking synergies bigger and faster than expected and
achieving a lower weighted average cost of capital. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The company delivered $1.3&nbsp;billion of synergies in 2020 and expects to more than double that in 2021 by
achieving $2.7 to $3.0&nbsp;billion of synergies. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Looking ahead, the company expects total run rate cost synergies to reach approximately $7.5&nbsp;billion per
year &#150; up 25&nbsp;percent from the original merger guidance of $6&nbsp;billion &#150; largely driven by greater efficiencies in site costs and marketing expenses, along with additional information technology savings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Delivering Even Better Financial Results &#150; </B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is
raising <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-term</FONT> and long-term guidance across the board with higher service revenue, higher Core Adjusted EBITDA and higher free cash flow &#150; setting up the flexibility for substantial shareholder return
options with potentially up to $60&nbsp;billion in shareholder return between 2023 to 2025. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Service revenue is expected to be $61&nbsp;billion to $62&nbsp;billion in 2023 &#150; up $1.5&nbsp;billion at the
midpoint from the original guidance. Long-term, service revenue is expected to be over $70&nbsp;billion by 2026 &#150; above the top of the range in the original guidance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Core adjusted EBITDA is expected to be $28&nbsp;billion to $29&nbsp;billion in 2023 compared to the original
guidance which implied $25&nbsp;billion to $27&nbsp;billion &#150; a $2.5&nbsp;billion increase at the midpoint. Long-term, core adjusted EBITDA is expected to be more than $36&nbsp;billion by 2026 &#150; $1&nbsp;billion above the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">high-end</FONT> of the original guidance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Free cash flow is expected to be $13&nbsp;billion to $14&nbsp;billion in 2023 &#150; up $3&nbsp;billion from the
original guidance. Long-term, free cash flow is expected to be more than $18&nbsp;billion by 2026 &#150; above the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">high-end</FONT> of the original guidance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> U.S. Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is America&#146;s supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT>
delivering an advanced 4G LTE and transformative nationwide 5G network that will offer reliable connectivity for all. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> customers benefit from its unmatched combination of value and quality,
unwavering obsession with offering them the best possible service experience and undisputable drive for disruption that creates competition and innovation in wireless and beyond. Based in Bellevue, Wash.,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint. For
more information please visit:&nbsp;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://www.t-mobile.com</FONT></U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Forward-Looking Statements

Interest expense. Core Adjusted EBITDA should not be used to predict Net income as the difference between the Core Adjusted EBITDA and Net income is variable. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This guidance was prepared based on internal forecasts and models prior to the Company&#146;s adoption of ASU <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2016-15,</FONT> &#147;Statement of Cash Flows (Topic 230): Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments&#148; which impacted the presentation of (1)&nbsp;cash flows related to beneficial interests in
securitization transactions resulting in a reclassification of cash inflows from Operating activities to Investing activities and (2)&nbsp;cash payments for debt prepayment or debt extinguishment costs resulting in a reclassification of cash
outflows from Operating activities to Financing activities. As a result, at the time the guidance was publicly released in April 2018, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> was not able to forecast GAAP Net cash provided by operating
activities on a forward-looking basis without unreasonable efforts due to the Company&#146;s adoption of ASU <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2016-15</FONT> on January&nbsp;1, 2018. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Definitions of Terms </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Adjusted EBITDA
and Core Adjusted EBITDA</B> - Adjusted EBITDA represents earnings before Interest expense, net of Interest income, Income tax expense, Depreciation and amortization expense, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> Stock-based compensation
and certain expenses not reflective of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> ongoing operating performance, such as Merger-related costs,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19-related</FONT></FONT> costs and Impairment expense. Core Adjusted EBITDA represents Adjusted EBITDA less Lease Revenues. Core Adjusted EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA are <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures utilized by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> management to monitor the financial performance of our operations. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT>
uses Core Adjusted EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA as benchmarks to evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> operating performance in comparison to its competitors. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> also uses
Adjusted EBITDA internally as a measure to evaluate and compensate its personnel and management for their performance. Management believes analysts and investors use Core Adjusted EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA as supplemental measures to evaluate
overall operating performance and facilitate comparisons with other wireless communications companies because they are indicative of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> ongoing operating performance and trends by excluding the
impact of Interest expense from financing, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> depreciation and amortization from capital investments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> stock-based compensation, Merger-related costs
including network decommissioning costs, incremental costs directly attributable to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> and impairment expense, as they are not indicative of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT>
ongoing operating performance, as well as certain other nonrecurring income and expenses. Management believes analysts and investors use Core Adjusted EBITDA because it normalizes for the transition in the company&#146;s device financing strategy,
by excluding the impact of lease revenues from Adjusted EBITDA, to align with the related depreciation expense on leased devices, which is excluded from the definition of Adjusted EBITDA. Core Adjusted EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA have limitations as
analytical tools and should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for income from operations, Net income or any other measure of financial performance reported in accordance with U.S. Generally Accepted Accounting Principles
(&#147;GAAP&#148;). </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Free Cash Flow</B> - Net cash provided by operating activities less cash purchases of property and
equipment, including proceeds from sales of tower sites and proceeds related to beneficial interests in securitization transactions and less cash payments for debt prepayment or debt extinguishment costs. Free Cash Flow is utilized by <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> management, investors, and analysts to evaluate cash available to pay debt and provide further investment in the business. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>
